#+title: Ethereum RPC2 API
#+author: zven

* Ethereum API
** [[https://infura.io/docs/ethereum#operation/web3_clientVersion][web3_clientVersion]]
Returns the version of the current client.
#+begin_src restclient
POST https://data-seed-prebsc-1-s1.binance.org:8545/
Content-Type: application/json
{
    "id": "1337",
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "web3_clientVersion"
}

#+end_src

** web3_sha3
Hashes data using the Keccak-256 algorithm
#+begin_src restclient
POST https://data-seed-prebsc-1-s1.binance.org:8545/
Content-Type: application/json
{
    "id": "1337",
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "web3_sha3",
    "params": ["0x01"]
}

#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
#+BEGIN_SRC js
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": "1337",
  "result": "0x5fe7f977e71dba2ea1a68e21057beebb9be2ac30c6410aa38d4f3fbe41dcffd2"
}

// POST https://data-seed-prebsc-1-s1.binance.org:8545/
// HTTP/1.1 200 OK
// Date: Tue, 13 Jul 2021 08:29:37 GMT
// Content-Type: application/json
// Content-Length: 118
// Connection: close
// Vary: Origin
// Request duration: 0.762797s
#+END_SRC

#+end_src

** net_listening
Determines if this client is listening for new network connections
#+begin_src restclient
POST https://data-seed-prebsc-1-s1.binance.org:8545/
Content-Type: application/json
{
    "id": "1337",
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "net_listening"
}
#+end_src

#+RESULTS:
#+BEGIN_SRC js
{
  "jsonrpc": "2.0",
  "id": "1337",
  "result": true
}

// POST https://data-seed-prebsc-1-s1.binance.org:8545/
// HTTP/1.1 200 OK
// Date: Tue, 13 Jul 2021 08:32:54 GMT
// Content-Type: application/json
// Content-Length: 68
// Connection: close
// Vary: Origin
// Request duration: 0.849160s
#+END_SRC

** TODO eth_sendTransaction
Creates, signs, and sends a new transaction to the network
#+begin_src restclient
POST https://data-seed-prebsc-1-s1.binance.org:8545/
Content-Type: application/json
{
    "id": "1337",
    "jsonrpc": "2.0",
    "method": "eth_sendTransaction",
    "params": [
        {
        "data":"0x60084bd2CCF3F3f8D821e109bf7b4bE836683Bd1",
        "from":"0x407d73d8a49eeb85d32cf465507dd71d507100c1",
        "gas":"0xe8",
        "gasPrice":"0xe8",
        "to":"0xe4a0c9a1b6c3305B931a8cf4845F175d3f96CEe8",
        "value":"0xe8"
        }
    ]
}

#+end_src
